<Time>1468296495057< /Time><user_id>110154708357398947388< /user_id><rate>4< /rate>< username>
Dan Seguin<//username>
<Text>Had my dog with me and some time to kill while waiting to give a ride to a friend, so thought I'd do some some exploring. Saw the sign and entered a rather unassuming parking lot with no expectations. Both dog and I ended up really enjoying ourselves. Just past the small rectangular lot with parking and concrete picnic tables on one side, a sandy trail snaked through some low brush and through a cut in the small hill to reveal several rows of  20-40' sand  dunes dotted with clusters of brush as far as the eye could see in one direction, and perhaps 3-4 large dunes and valleys between the trailhead and the beach (which I never made it too). Instead I climbed the sliding face of one of the closest tallest dunes (not easy) and rested under a wind-swept tree along it's winding peak. It was a very bizarre sight, one side of this mount was pristine white sand and scrub, but the backside descended into a loamy, shady, forested area, that descended another 40' below the dune's base down to a set of trails that cris-crossed a dry stream bed. Time was up for exploring, but I'll definitely be back, next time allotting more exploration time. Lastly, you might think an area like that with it's many private hidden spots might be populated with transients and littered with trash, but none of either was to be seen. A potential nice place to get away with someone for an afternoon and find a fun spot to relax.</Text>< Response>
None</Response>

<username>S</username><time>1533096052799<//time><Rating>3</Rating>< Text>
I would actually give them a 2.5. Sometimes they are awesome; the food is hot, well made, and delivered in a reasonable amount of time. Sometimes the food is warm, not terribly made and the delivery time is too long. Sometimes the food is cold, inedible, and takes a ridiculous amount of time to be delivered. I live approximately a 5 - 7 minute drive from the store and the food never arrives in less than 20 minutes of being "out for delivery." Sometimes it takes more than an hour to arrive. That being said the absolute worst part about this store is the customer service. The delivery people are generally ok to awesome. The people in the store tend to be just awful. I only call the store when my food is taking way too long to be delivered or is inedible. To their credit, they always offer to remake my order and send it out free of additional charge, if it is inedible. Once in a while the person I talk to in genuinely nice. However, generally when I call in all I receive are excuses and a begrudging offer of store credit if I request a refund for food I can't eat. Not once has anyone taken responsibility for the problems. Not even the manager. All blame is passed on to the main/general/head manager. Pretty sure this "manager" is a fictional scapegoat because he is never in. I'm always told to "call back tomorrow." Not once has anyone admitted to "him" being at work. Hopefully if you order from this store you catch them on a good day.< /Text>
